Source: http://spr.com/building-a-simple-rest-api-with-scala-play-part-1/

How to make it work in eclipse:
-. https://github.com/typesafehub/sbteclipse

How to make it work in docker:
http://blog.jaceklaskowski.pl/2015/07/24/docker-your-scala-web-application-play-framework.html

list of useful docker commands:
sbt docker:publishLocal
docker run --name mangafun -p 8080:9000 deadbolt-2-usage-scala:2.5.0
=> now you can access your app from http://localhost:8080
then:
docker images
docker container prune
docker image rm <image-id-from-running docker images>

https://stackoverflow.com/a/24850114/474330
sbt docker:stage
cd target/docker/stage
docker build .

List[Future[String]] => Future[List[String]]
https://stackoverflow.com/a/20012490/474330
